19 ! Adapted for DFTB+ from John Burkardt's portation of Dmitri Laikov's
20 ! C implementation of
21 !
22 ! V.I. Lebedev, and D.N. Laikov, "A quadrature formula for the sphere of the
23 ! 131st algebraic order of accuracy", Doklady Mathematics, Vol. 59, No. 3,
24 ! 1999, pp. 477-481.
25 module xtb_solv_lebedev
26  use xtb_mctc_accuracy, only : wp
27  implicit none
28 
29  private
30 
31  public :: gridsize
32  public :: getanggrid
33 
35  integer, parameter :: gridsize(32) = [ &
36  & 6, 14, 26, 38, 50, 74, 86, 110, &
37  & 146, 170, 194, 230, 266, 302, 350, 434, &
38  & 590, 770, 974, 1202, 1454, 1730, 2030, 2354, &
39  & 2702, 3074, 3470, 3890, 4334, 4802, 5294, 5810]
40 
41  real(wp), parameter :: z = 0.0_wp
42 
43 
44 contains
45 
46 
48 pure subroutine getanggrid(nAng, grid, weights, stat)
49 
51  integer, intent(in) :: nang
52 
54  real(wp), intent(out) :: grid(:, :)
55 
57  real(wp), intent(out) :: weights(:)
58 
60  integer, intent(out) :: stat
61 
62  integer :: np
63 
64  grid(:, :) = 0.0_wp
65  weights(:) = 0.0_wp
66 
67  if (nang <= 0 .or. nang > size(gridsize)) then
68  stat = 1
69  return
70  end if
71 
72  if (size(grid, dim=1) /= 3 .or. size(grid, dim=2) < gridsize(nang)) then
73  stat = 2
74  return
75  end if
76 
77  if (size(weights, dim=1) < gridsize(nang)) then
78  stat = 3
79  return
80  end if
81 
82  select case(nang)
83  case( 1); call ld0006(grid, weights, np)
84  case( 2); call ld0014(grid, weights, np)
85  case( 3); call ld0026(grid, weights, np)
86  case( 4); call ld0038(grid, weights, np)
87  case( 5); call ld0050(grid, weights, np)
88  case( 6); call ld0074(grid, weights, np)
89  case( 7); call ld0086(grid, weights, np)
90  case( 8); call ld0110(grid, weights, np)
91  case( 9); call ld0146(grid, weights, np)
92  case(10); call ld0170(grid, weights, np)
93  case(11); call ld0194(grid, weights, np)
94  case(12); call ld0230(grid, weights, np)
95  case(13); call ld0266(grid, weights, np)
96  case(14); call ld0302(grid, weights, np)
97  case(15); call ld0350(grid, weights, np)
98  case(16); call ld0434(grid, weights, np)
99  case(17); call ld0590(grid, weights, np)
100  case(18); call ld0770(grid, weights, np)
101  case(19); call ld0974(grid, weights, np)
102  case(20); call ld1202(grid, weights, np)
103  case(21); call ld1454(grid, weights, np)
104  case(22); call ld1730(grid, weights, np)
105  case(23); call ld2030(grid, weights, np)
106  case(24); call ld2354(grid, weights, np)
107  case(25); call ld2702(grid, weights, np)
108  case(26); call ld3074(grid, weights, np)
109  case(27); call ld3470(grid, weights, np)
110  case(28); call ld3890(grid, weights, np)
111  case(29); call ld4334(grid, weights, np)
112  case(30); call ld4802(grid, weights, np)
113  case(31); call ld5294(grid, weights, np)
114  case(32); call ld5810(grid, weights, np)
115  end select
116 
117  if (np == gridsize(nang)) then
118  stat = 0
119  else
120  stat = -1
121  end if
122 
123 end subroutine getanggrid
124 
126 pure subroutine genoh1(num, x, w, v)
127  integer, intent(inout) :: num
128  real(wp),intent(inout) :: x(3,*)
129  real(wp),intent(inout) :: w(*)
130  real(wp),intent(in) :: v
131  real(wp) :: a
132  a = 1.0_wp
133  x(:,1) = [ a, z, z]
134  x(:,2) = [-a, z, z]
135  x(:,3) = [ z, a, z]
136  x(:,4) = [ z, -a, z]
137  x(:,5) = [ z, z, a]
138  x(:,6) = [ z, z, -a]
139  w(1:6) = v
140  num = num+6
141 end subroutine genoh1
142 
144 pure subroutine genoh2(num, x, w, v)
145  integer, intent(inout) :: num
146  real(wp),intent(inout) :: x(3,*)
147  real(wp),intent(inout) :: w(*)
148  real(wp),intent(in) :: v
149  real(wp) :: a
150  a = sqrt(0.5_wp)
151  x(:, 1) = [ z, a, a]
152  x(:, 2) = [ z, -a, a]
153  x(:, 3) = [ z, a, -a]
154  x(:, 4) = [ z, -a, -a]
155  x(:, 5) = [ a, z, a]
156  x(:, 6) = [-a, z, a]
157  x(:, 7) = [ a, z, -a]
158  x(:, 8) = [-a, z, -a]
159  x(:, 9) = [ a, a, z]
160  x(:,10) = [-a, a, z]
161  x(:,11) = [ a, -a, z]
162  x(:,12) = [-a, -a, z]
163  w(1:12) = v
164  num = num+12
165 end subroutine genoh2
166 
168 pure subroutine genoh3(num, x, w, v)
169  integer, intent(inout) :: num
170  real(wp),intent(inout) :: x(3,*)
171  real(wp),intent(inout) :: w(*)
172  real(wp),intent(in) :: v
173  real(wp) :: a
174  a = sqrt(1._wp/3._wp)
175  x(:,1) = [ a, a, a]
176  x(:,2) = [-a, a, a]
177  x(:,3) = [ a, -a, a]
178  x(:,4) = [-a, -a, a]
179  x(:,5) = [ a, a, -a]
180  x(:,6) = [-a, a, -a]
181  x(:,7) = [ a, -a, -a]
182  x(:,8) = [-a, -a, -a]
183  w(1:8) = v
184  num = num+8
185 end subroutine genoh3
186 
188 pure subroutine genoh4(num, x, w, a, v)
189  integer, intent(inout) :: num
190  real(wp),intent(inout) :: x(3,*)
191  real(wp),intent(inout) :: w(*)
192  real(wp),intent(in) :: a, v
193  real(wp) :: b
194  b = sqrt(1._wp - 2._wp*a*a)
195  x(:, 1) = [ a, a, b]
196  x(:, 2) = [-a, a, b]
197  x(:, 3) = [ a, -a, b]
198  x(:, 4) = [-a, -a, b]
199  x(:, 5) = [ a, a, -b]
200  x(:, 6) = [-a, a, -b]
201  x(:, 7) = [ a, -a, -b]
202  x(:, 8) = [-a, -a, -b]
203  x(:, 9) = [ a, b, a]
204  x(:,10) = [-a, b, a]
205  x(:,11) = [ a, -b, a]
206  x(:,12) = [-a, -b, a]
207  x(:,13) = [ a, b, -a]
208  x(:,14) = [-a, b, -a]
209  x(:,15) = [ a, -b, -a]
210  x(:,16) = [-a, -b, -a]
211  x(:,17) = [ b, a, a]
212  x(:,18) = [-b, a, a]
213  x(:,19) = [ b, -a, a]
214  x(:,20) = [-b, -a, a]
215  x(:,21) = [ b, a, -a]
216  x(:,22) = [-b, a, -a]
217  x(:,23) = [ b, -a, -a]
218  x(:,24) = [-b, -a, -a]
219  w(1:24) = v
220  num = num+24
221 end subroutine genoh4
222 
224 pure subroutine genoh5(num, x, w, a, v)
225  integer, intent(inout) :: num
226  real(wp),intent(inout) :: x(3,*)
227  real(wp),intent(inout) :: w(*)
228  real(wp),intent(in) :: a, v
229  real(wp) :: b
230  b = sqrt(1.0_wp-a*a)
231  x(:, 1) = [ a, b, z]
232  x(:, 2) = [-a, b, z]
233  x(:, 3) = [ a, -b, z]
234  x(:, 4) = [-a, -b, z]
235  x(:, 5) = [ b, a, z]
236  x(:, 6) = [-b, a, z]
237  x(:, 7) = [ b, -a, z]
238  x(:, 8) = [-b, -a, z]
239  x(:, 9) = [ a, z, b]
240  x(:,10) = [-a, z, b]
241  x(:,11) = [ a, z, -b]
242  x(:,12) = [-a, z, -b]
243  x(:,13) = [ b, z, a]
244  x(:,14) = [-b, z, a]
245  x(:,15) = [ b, z, -a]
246  x(:,16) = [-b, z, -a]
247  x(:,17) = [ z, a, b]
248  x(:,18) = [ z, -a, b]
249  x(:,19) = [ z, a, -b]
250  x(:,20) = [ z, -a, -b]
251  x(:,21) = [ z, b, a]
252  x(:,22) = [ z, -b, a]
253  x(:,23) = [ z, b, -a]
254  x(:,24) = [ z, -b, -a]
255  w(1:24) = v
256  num = num+24
257 end subroutine genoh5

260 pure subroutine genoh6(num, x, w, a, b, v)
261  integer, intent(inout) :: num
262  real(wp),intent(inout) :: x(3,*)
263  real(wp),intent(inout) :: w(*)
264  real(wp),intent(in) :: a, b, v
265  real(wp) :: c
266  c = sqrt(1._wp - a*a - b*b)
267  x(:, 1) = [ a, b, c]
268  x(:, 2) = [-a, b, c]
269  x(:, 3) = [ a, -b, c]
270  x(:, 4) = [-a, -b, c]
271  x(:, 5) = [ a, b, -c]
272  x(:, 6) = [-a, b, -c]
273  x(:, 7) = [ a, -b, -c]
274  x(:, 8) = [-a, -b, -c]
275  x(:, 9) = [ a, c, b]
276  x(:,10) = [-a, c, b]
277  x(:,11) = [ a, -c, b]
278  x(:,12) = [-a, -c, b]
279  x(:,13) = [ a, c, -b]
280  x(:,14) = [-a, c, -b]
281  x(:,15) = [ a, -c, -b]
282  x(:,16) = [-a, -c, -b]
283  x(:,17) = [ b, a, c]
284  x(:,18) = [-b, a, c]
285  x(:,19) = [ b, -a, c]
286  x(:,20) = [-b, -a, c]
287  x(:,21) = [ b, a, -c]
288  x(:,22) = [-b, a, -c]
289  x(:,23) = [ b, -a, -c]
290  x(:,24) = [-b, -a, -c]
291  x(:,25) = [ b, c, a]
292  x(:,26) = [-b, c, a]
293  x(:,27) = [ b, -c, a]
294  x(:,28) = [-b, -c, a]
295  x(:,29) = [ b, c, -a]
296  x(:,30) = [-b, c, -a]
297  x(:,31) = [ b, -c, -a]
298  x(:,32) = [-b, -c, -a]
299  x(:,33) = [ c, a, b]
300  x(:,34) = [-c, a, b]
301  x(:,35) = [ c, -a, b]
302  x(:,36) = [-c, -a, b]
303  x(:,37) = [ c, a, -b]
304  x(:,38) = [-c, a, -b]
305  x(:,39) = [ c, -a, -b]
306  x(:,40) = [-c, -a, -b]
307  x(:,41) = [ c, b, a]
308  x(:,42) = [-c, b, a]
309  x(:,43) = [ c, -b, a]
310  x(:,44) = [-c, -b, a]
311  x(:,45) = [ c, b, -a]
312  x(:,46) = [-c, b, -a]
313  x(:,47) = [ c, -b, -a]
314  x(:,48) = [-c, -b, -a]
315  w(1:48) = v
316  num = num+48
317 end subroutine genoh6

319 pure subroutine ld0006(x, w, n)
320  real(wp),intent(out) :: x(3, 6), w(6)
321  integer, intent(out) :: n
322  real(wp) :: a,b,v
323  n = 1
324  v = 0.1666666666666667e+0_wp
325  call genoh1(n, x(1, n), w(n), v)
326  n = n-1
327 end subroutine ld0006
328
